\DoxyCodeLine{00538\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ Adjust\ format\ string\ to\ decorate\ the\ value\ with\ a\ prefix,\ a\ suffix,\ or\ adapt\ the\ editing\ and\ display\ precision\ e.g.\ "{}\%.3f"{}\ -\/>\ 1.234;\ "{}\%5.2f\ secs"{}\ -\/>\ 01.23\ secs;\ "{}Biscuit:\ \%.0f"{}\ -\/>\ Biscuit:\ 1;\ etc.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00540\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ Speed\ are\ per-\/pixel\ of\ mouse\ movement\ (v\_speed=0.2f:\ mouse\ needs\ to\ move\ by\ 5\ pixels\ to\ increase\ value\ by\ 1).\ For\ gamepad/keyboard\ navigation,\ minimum\ speed\ is\ Max(v\_speed,\ minimum\_step\_at\_given\_precision).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00541\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ Use\ v\_min\ <\ v\_max\ to\ clamp\ edits\ to\ given\ limits.\ Note\ that\ CTRL+Click\ manual\ input\ can\ override\ those\ limits\ if\ ImGuiSliderFlags\_AlwaysClamp\ is\ not\ used.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00542\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ Use\ v\_max\ =\ FLT\_MAX\ /\ INT\_MAX\ etc\ to\ avoid\ clamping\ to\ a\ maximum,\ same\ with\ v\_min\ =\ -\/FLT\_MAX\ /\ INT\_MIN\ to\ avoid\ clamping\ to\ a\ minimum.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00733\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Tables}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00734\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ Full-\/featured\ replacement\ for\ old\ Columns\ API.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00735\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ See\ Demo-\/>Tables\ for\ demo\ code.\ See\ top\ of\ imgui\_tables.cpp\ for\ general\ commentary.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00736\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ See\ ImGuiTableFlags\_\ and\ ImGuiTableColumnFlags\_\ enums\ for\ a\ description\ of\ available\ flags.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00737\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ The\ typical\ call\ flow\ is:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00738\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ 1.\ Call\ BeginTable(),\ early\ out\ if\ returning\ false.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00739\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ 2.\ Optionally\ call\ TableSetupColumn()\ to\ submit\ column\ name/flags/defaults.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00740\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ 3.\ Optionally\ call\ TableSetupScrollFreeze()\ to\ request\ scroll\ freezing\ of\ columns/rows.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00741\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ 4.\ Optionally\ call\ TableHeadersRow()\ to\ submit\ a\ header\ row.\ Names\ are\ pulled\ from\ TableSetupColumn()\ data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00742\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ 5.\ Populate\ contents:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00743\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ In\ most\ situations\ you\ can\ use\ TableNextRow()\ +\ TableSetColumnIndex(N)\ to\ start\ appending\ into\ a\ column.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00744\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ If\ you\ are\ using\ tables\ as\ a\ sort\ of\ grid,\ where\ every\ column\ is\ holding\ the\ same\ type\ of\ contents,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00745\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ you\ may\ prefer\ using\ TableNextColumn()\ instead\ of\ TableNextRow()\ +\ TableSetColumnIndex().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00746\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ TableNextColumn()\ will\ automatically\ wrap-\/around\ into\ the\ next\ row\ if\ needed.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00747\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ IMPORTANT:\ Comparatively\ to\ the\ old\ Columns()\ API,\ we\ need\ to\ call\ TableNextColumn()\ for\ the\ first\ column!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00748\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ Summary\ of\ possible\ call\ flow:}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00750\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ TableNextRow()\ -\/>\ TableSetColumnIndex(0)\ -\/>\ Text("{}Hello\ 0"{})\ -\/>\ TableSetColumnIndex(1)\ -\/>\ Text("{}Hello\ 1"{})\ \ //\ OK}}

\DoxyCodeLine{01148\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Flags\ for\ ImGui::BeginTable()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01149\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ Important!\ Sizing\ policies\ have\ complex\ and\ subtle\ side\ effects,\ much\ more\ so\ than\ you\ would\ expect.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01150\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ Read\ comments/demos\ carefully\ +\ experiment\ with\ live\ demos\ to\ get\ acquainted\ with\ them.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01151\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ The\ DEFAULT\ sizing\ policies\ are:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01152\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ Default\ to\ ImGuiTableFlags\_SizingFixedFit\ \ \ \ if\ ScrollX\ is\ on,\ or\ if\ host\ window\ has\ ImGuiWindowFlags\_AlwaysAutoResize.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01153\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ Default\ to\ ImGuiTableFlags\_SizingStretchSame\ if\ ScrollX\ is\ off.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01154\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ When\ ScrollX\ is\ off:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01155\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ Table\ defaults\ to\ ImGuiTableFlags\_SizingStretchSame\ -\/>\ all\ Columns\ defaults\ to\ ImGuiTableColumnFlags\_WidthStretch\ with\ same\ weight.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01156\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ Columns\ sizing\ policy\ allowed:\ Stretch\ (default),\ Fixed/Auto.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01157\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ Fixed\ Columns\ (if\ any)\ will\ generally\ obtain\ their\ requested\ width\ (unless\ the\ table\ cannot\ fit\ them\ all).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01158\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ Stretch\ Columns\ will\ share\ the\ remaining\ width\ according\ to\ their\ respective\ weight.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01159\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ Mixed\ Fixed/Stretch\ columns\ is\ possible\ but\ has\ various\ side-\/effects\ on\ resizing\ behaviors.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01160\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ The\ typical\ use\ of\ mixing\ sizing\ policies\ is:\ any\ number\ of\ LEADING\ Fixed\ columns,\ followed\ by\ one\ or\ two\ TRAILING\ Stretch\ columns.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01161\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ (this\ is\ because\ the\ visible\ order\ of\ columns\ have\ subtle\ but\ necessary\ effects\ on\ how\ they\ react\ to\ manual\ resizing).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01162\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ When\ ScrollX\ is\ on:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01163\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ Table\ defaults\ to\ ImGuiTableFlags\_SizingFixedFit\ -\/>\ all\ Columns\ defaults\ to\ ImGuiTableColumnFlags\_WidthFixed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01164\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ Columns\ sizing\ policy\ allowed:\ Fixed/Auto\ mostly.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01165\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ Fixed\ Columns\ can\ be\ enlarged\ as\ needed.\ Table\ will\ show\ a\ horizontal\ scrollbar\ if\ needed.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01166\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ When\ using\ auto-\/resizing\ (non-\/resizable)\ fixed\ columns,\ querying\ the\ content\ width\ to\ use\ item\ right-\/alignment\ e.g.\ SetNextItemWidth(-\/FLT\_MIN)\ doesn't\ make\ sense,\ would\ create\ a\ feedback\ loop.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01167\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ Using\ Stretch\ columns\ OFTEN\ DOES\ NOT\ MAKE\ SENSE\ if\ ScrollX\ is\ on,\ UNLESS\ you\ have\ specified\ a\ value\ for\ 'inner\_width'\ in\ BeginTable().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01168\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ If\ you\ specify\ a\ value\ for\ 'inner\_width'\ then\ effectively\ the\ scrolling\ space\ is\ known\ and\ Stretch\ or\ mixed\ Fixed/Stretch\ columns\ become\ meaningful\ again.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01169\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ Read\ on\ documentation\ at\ the\ top\ of\ imgui\_tables.cpp\ for\ details.}}
